    function noxfs() {
        try {
            if (window.top !== window.self) {
                document.write = "";
                window.top.location = window.self.location;
                setTimeout(function() {
                    document.body.innerHTML = '';
                }, 0);
                window.self.onload = function() {
                    document.body.innerHTML = '';
                };
            }
        } catch (err) {
        }
    }
    noxfs();
    window.onerror = function(message, file, line) {
      try{
       var sFormattedMessage = '[' + file + ' (' + line + ')] ' + message;
       _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Exceptions', 'JS errors', sFormattedMessage, null, true]);
      }
      catch(e){}
    };

    function addEvent(elm, evType, fn, useCapture) {
        useCapture = useCapture || false;
        if (elm.addEventListener) {
            elm.addEventListener(evType, fn, false);
            return true;
        } else if (elm.attachEvent) {
            var r = elm.attachEvent('on' + evType, fn);
            return r;
        } else {
            elm['on' + evType] = fn;
        }
    };

    function removeEvent(elm, evType, fn, useCapture) {
        useCapture = useCapture || false;
        if (elm.removeEventListener){
            elm.removeEventListener(evType, fn, false);
        } else if (elm.detachEvent) {
             elm.detachEvent("on"+evType, fn);
        } else {
            delete elm["on"+evType];
        }
    };

    function setInteractTime() {
        window.T_INTERACT = (new Date()).getTime();
        removeEvent(window, 'click', setInteractTime);
        removeEvent(window, 'mousemove', setInteractTime);
        removeEvent(window, 'scroll', setInteractTime);
    }

    addEvent(window, 'click', setInteractTime);
    addEvent(window, 'mousemove', setInteractTime);
    addEvent(window, 'scroll', setInteractTime);

</script>

        <script type="text/javascript+fk-onload">
            (function() {

                var dialogEl = $('#track-order-details-content'),
                    emailEl = dialogEl.find(".email-id"),
                    orderEl = dialogEl.find(".order-id"),
                    errorEl = dialogEl.find(".fk-err-all"),
                    errorWrapEl = dialogEl.find(".fk-error-all-wrap"),
                    orderDetailsForm = $("form[name=order-details-form]"),
                    orderIdSubText = $(".sub-text-order-id");

                $(".track-order-details-required").on("click", function() {
                    var dialog,
                        href = "/account/orders";

                    dialog = new FKART.ui.Dialog({
                        body: dialogEl,
                        width: 746,
                        cssClass: "track-order-details-dialog"
                    });

                    orderDetailsForm.on("submit", function() {
                        var emailId = emailEl.val(),
                            orderId = orderEl.val();

                        $.ajax({
                            url: "/xhr/getUserOrderDetails",
                            dataType: "json",
                            type: "POST",
                            data: {
                                "emailId": emailId,
                                "orderId": orderId
                            },
                            success: function(data) {
                                if(data && data.success) {
                                    window.location.href = data.redirectUrl;
                                } else {
                                    errorEl.text(data.error);
                                    errorWrapEl.show();
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    });

                    dialogEl.on("click", ".login", function() {
                        dialog.hide();
                        FKART.login.showPopup(href);
                    });

                    orderEl.on("keyup", function(){
                        var currLength = parseInt(orderEl.val().length, 10),
                            availLength = 13 - currLength,
                            subText;

                        if(currLength === 0){
                            subText = "13 characters";
                        } else {
                            subText = availLength + " characters remaining";
                        }

                        orderIdSubText.text(subText);
                    });

                    dialog.show();
                    return false;
                });
            })();
        </script>

<script type="text/javascript+fk-onload">
<!--<script type="text/javascript">-->

    var searchOptionUrls = {"all":"\/all","clothing":"\/clothing","footwear":"\/footwear","mobiles":"\/mobiles","computers":"\/computers","leather-travel":"\/lifestyle\/bags-belts-luggage","cameras":"\/cameras","books-stationeries":"\/books-stationeries","homeappliance":"\/home-appliances","health-and-beauty":"\/health-and-beauty","games":"\/games","tv-video":"\/tv-video","audioplayers":"\/audio","movies-music":"\/movies-music","babycaretoys":"\/babycaretoies","sports-fitness":"\/sports-fitness","ebooks":"\/ebooks"};
    function submitSearchBarForm(){
        var sb = $(".search-bar-text"),
            val = sb.val();

        val = val.replace(/^[ ]+/g, "").replace(/[ ]+$/g, "");
        if(val === "" || val.toLowerCase() == "Search for a product, category or brand"){
            sb.focus();
            return false;
        }
        return true;
    };

    function formatItem(row) {
        return row;
    };

    $(".search-bar-text")
        .keypress(function(event){
            if(event.keyCode == 13 && $("#fk-vertical-auto-suggestions").val()!="search.flipkart.com"){
                var vertical = $("#fk-vertical-auto-suggestions").val();
                window.location.href = searchOptionUrls[vertical];
                return;
            }
        }).autocomplete("/s", {
            max: 12,
            minChars: 1,
            scroll: false,
            selectFirst: false,
            formatItem:formatItem,
            delay: 100        });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript+fk-onload">
    (function() {
        var stickyMenu = _.throttle(updateMenuPosition, 200);
        var menuTimer = null;
        var isMenuOpen = false;
        $('.menu-l0','.menubar').mouseenter(function(){
            menuTimer = setTimeout(openMenu,200);
        });
        $('.menubar').mouseleave(function(){
            clearTimeout(menuTimer);
            menuTimer = null;
            $('.menubar').addClass('slowMenu');
        });
        var openMenu = function(){
            isMenuOpen = true;
            $('.menubar').removeClass('slowMenu');
        }
        $('.submenu').mouseenter(function(){
            $('.menu-header-content').addClass('zeroTopMargin');
        });
        $('.submenu').mouseleave(function(){
            $('.menu-header-content').removeClass('zeroTopMargin hide');
        });
        var $window = $(window);
        var $menu = $(".menubar");
        var $menuBar = $('.menu-header-content');
        var $topBar = $('.header-topbar');
        var $topBar_text = $topBar.find(".text");
        var $headerLinks = $('.header-links');
        var isMenuSticking = false;
        var lastScrollTop = 0;
        function updateMenuPosition() {
            requestAnimFrame(function(){
                    var st = $window.scrollTop();
            if(st < lastScrollTop) {
                //upscroll
                if(st<60 && isMenuSticking) {
                        $menu.trigger("sticky-end");
                        isMenuSticking = false;
                        $menuBar.hasClass("hide") && $menuBar.removeClass('hide');
                }
                if(st < lastScrollTop - 400){
                   $menuBar.hasClass("hide") && $menuBar.removeClass('hide');

                }
            } else {
                //downscroll
                if(st>=70) {
                    // we have to show the menu when scrool to top is 70px
                    !$menuBar.hasClass("hide") && $menuBar.addClass('hide');
                    if(!isMenuSticking){
                        $menu.trigger("sticky-start");
                        isMenuSticking = true;
                    }
                }
            }
            lastScrollTop = st;
            });
        }

        $("[data-lazy-src]",'.submenu').each(function(){
            var object = $(this).attr('data-lazy-src');
            $(this).attr('src', object);
            $(this).removeAttr('data-lazy-src');  
        });

        $menu.bind("sticky-start", function() {
            $topBar.addClass('smaller');
            $topBar_text.hide();
        });

        $menu.bind("sticky-end", function() {
            $topBar.removeClass('smaller');
            setTimeout(function(){$topBar_text.show();},300);
        });

        function try_persist() {
            if(window.localStorage) {
                var ls_success = true;
                $(".menu-l0 .submenu").each(function(){
                    var key = "submenu_html-"+$(this).data("submenu-key");
                    try{
                      window.localStorage.setItem(key, $(this).html() );
                    } catch(e) {
                        ls_success = false;
                        return false;
                    }
                });
                ls_success && $.cookie("ft-ls", "1", { expires: new Date(new Date().getTime() + 10 * 60 * 1000), path:"/" });
            }
        }

       function menu_init() {
           $(".menu_docwrite").remove();
                          !$.cookie("ft-ls") && try_persist();
                       $(".menu-l0 .submenu").each(function() {
                var tabs = $(this).tabs().data("tabs_instance");
                $(this).find('.tab').delayedHover(function(){
                    tabs.changeTab(this);
                },function(){},200);
            });
            $window.bind('scroll', stickyMenu);
       }

       function fetchAndUpdateMenu(cb) {
           var promise = $.getJSON("/xhr/getNewMenuHtml");
           promise.done(function(response){
               for(var key in response) {
                  $("#submenu_"+key).html(response[key]);
               }
               cb && cb();
           });
       }

       if(window.DWMM){
           $.cookie("ft-ls", "1", { expires: new Date(new Date().getTime() - 100), path:"/" });
           fetchAndUpdateMenu(menu_init)
       } else {
           menu_init();
       }
    })();
</script>
</div>

<script type="text/javascript+fk-onload">
    (function(){
        var tooltip;
        function submitSearchFeedback(data,ele){
            var req = $.post("/search/submitSearchRating",data, function(){
                ele.closest(".panel-search-rate").text("Thank you for your feedback!");
            });
            req.fail(function(){
                ele.closest(".panel-search-rate").text("Oops! some error occurred");
            })
        }
        function getSearchFeedbackData(){
            var query = $("#search-query").attr("value") || $("#fk-top-search-box").attr("value");
            var sid= s.getQueryParam("sid") || $("input#sid").val();
            return {"sid":sid,"query":query};

        }
        $(".fk-search-rate").click(function(){
            var $ele = $(this);
            var data= getSearchFeedbackData();
            data["rate"] = $ele.attr("data-rate");
            if($ele.attr("data-rate") == 1){
                if (typeof tooltip != 'undefined' && typeof tooltip.hide != 'undefined') { tooltip.hide();}
                submitSearchFeedback(data,$ele);
            }
            if($ele.attr("data-rate") == 0){
                if(!tooltip){
                    tooltip = new FKART.ui.Tooltip({
                        message: $("#search_feedback_tooltip"),
                        nearElement: $ele,
                        align:"b-right",
                        showCloseIcon: true
                    });

                    tooltip.bindEvent("afterShow", function(){
                        var container = tooltip.getContainer();

                        $(".search-feedback-form", container).bind('submit', function(){
                            var data= getSearchFeedbackData();
                            data["rate"]  = 0;
                            data["mobile_no"] =  $("#feedback_mobile_no").val();
                            data["email_id"] =  $("#feedback_email_id").val();
                            data["comments"] = $("#feedback_comments").val();
                            data["category"] = $('#feedback_category').find(":selected").val();
                            submitSearchFeedback(data,$ele);
                            tooltip.hide();
                            return false;
                        });
                        $(".fk-ui-tooltip-close", container).click(function(){
                            var data= getSearchFeedbackData();

                            data["rate"] = 0;
                            submitSearchFeedback(data,$ele);
                            tooltip.hide();
                            return false;
                        });
                    });
                }
                tooltip.show();
            }
        });
    })();



</script>

            
            
            
        </div>

    <script type="text/javascript+fk-onload">
    //Delegate mouse enter events of browse summary element to results
    $(".browse-decide").delegate("[data-ratingfor]","mouseenter",function(){
        var _this = $(this);

        //data-browseSummaryLock maintains the information if the element is still hovered on
        _this.attr("data-browseSummaryLock","true");

        //Read product identifiers from attribute and then remove the attribute itself - so this handler wont be called on this element again
        var product_identifiers = _this.attr('data-ratingfor');
        //If ajax is already in progress for this product (indicated by data-ratingfor = AJAX_IN_PROGRESS), just return
        if(product_identifiers==="AJAX_IN_PROGRESS"){
            return;
        }

        if(product_identifiers && product_identifiers.split){
             //Split identifiers into individual values
             var identifiers = product_identifiers.split("#");
             //Indicate that the ajax for this attribute is in progress
             _this.attr("data-ratingfor","AJAX_IN_PROGRESS")
             $.get(
                "/ugc-ajax/getBrowseUGCSummary",
                {
                    item_id:identifiers[0],
                    product_id:identifiers[1],
                    product_title:identifiers[2]
                },
                function(response){
                    //Remove the attribute to stop calling hover on it.
                    _this.removeAttr("data-ratingfor");

                    //On successful ajax call, create the hover tooltip.
                    var tooltip = new FKART.ui.HoverTooltip({
                        message: response,
                        nearElement: _this,
                        align: "h-auto",
                        cssClass: "ugc-summary-tooltip",
                        showCloseIcon: false,
                        topGap : 55
                    });
                    //Read the lock (hover state) state and show tooltip if element is still hovered on
                    var lock = _this.attr("data-browseSummaryLock");
                    if(lock=="true"){
                        _this.trigger("mouseenter");

                        //Tracking code for popup open
                        var product_unit = _this.closest('[data-tracking-products]');
                        var productsVariable = product_unit.attr('data-tracking-products');
                        FKART.omni.customEvent("browse-decide-ugc: popup open",{products:productsVariable,events:"event10"});
                    }

                }
            );
        }

        _this.mouseleave(function(){
            //Remove lock to indicate that the hover state is no longer valid
            _this.removeAttr("data-browseSummaryLock");
        });
    });

    $("body").delegate("[data-browsedecide-tracking]","click",function(){
        var _this = $(this);

        var parentPopup = _this.closest("[data-ugc-summary-pid]");
        var pid = parentPopup.attr('data-ugc-summary-pid');
        var productVariableParent = $("[data-pid='"+pid+"'][data-tracking-products]");
        var productsVariable = productVariableParent.attr('data-tracking-products');
        var parameters = _this.attr("data-browsedecide-tracking");
        var omniture_data = parameters && parameters.split && parameters.split("#");
        var omni_data = {};
        if(omniture_data && omniture_data.length>0){

            var len = omniture_data.length;
            for(var index=0;index<len;index++){
                var paramValue = omniture_data[index];
                if(paramValue && paramValue.split){
                    paramValue = paramValue.split("=");
                    omni_data[paramValue[0]] = paramValue[1];
                }
            }
        }
        omni_data["products"]=productsVariable;
        omni_data["events"]="event91";
        FKART.omni.customEvent("browse-decide-ugc: click",omni_data);
    });

</script>

<script type="text/javascript+fk-onload">
(function(){
    function initiateChat(){
        var chatWin = window.open('', 'RightNowChat','toolbar=no, location=no, directories=no, status=no, resizable=yes, copyhistory=no, width=600, height=500,left=' + ((screen.width / 2) - 300) + ',top=' + ((screen.height / 2) - 300));
        try {
           chatWin.document && chatWin.document.write("<style>body { background-color: #E3F2F7; }</style><p style='position:absolute; font-weight:bold; left: 27%; top: 35%;'>Please wait while we are connecting to chat...</p>");
        } catch(e) { }
        chatWin.focus();
        FKART.loader.show();
        ajaxRequest('POST', '/assisted-buy/rightNowChat', {pageUrl: window.location.href}, {
            success:function (URL) {
                chatWin.location.href = URL;
                FKART.loader.hide();
            },
            error:function (msg, data) {
                if(msg == "User not logged in") {
                    FKART.login.showPopup(null,true);
                } else if(msg) {
                    new FKART.Alert({id:"error_chat", body:msg, destroy_on_close:true, width:500});
                }
                chatWin.close();
                FKART.loader.hide();
            }
        });
    }
    $('.assisted-buy-livechat').click(function(){
        initiateChat();
        FKART.omni.customEvent("Notifications", {'prop20':'AssistedBuy_livechat_click'});
    });
})();
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript+fk-onload">
        (function(){
            $(".login-required").on("click", function(e){
                showLoginTab();
            });
            $(".signup-link").on("click",function(){
               showSignupTab();
            });

            function showLoginTab(){
                $(".signup-button").removeClass('active');
                $(".login-button").addClass('active');
            }
            function showSignupTab(){
                $(".login-button").removeClass('active');
                $(".signup-button").addClass('active');
            }

            $(document).bind("login-initialized",function(){
                $(".login-button").click(function(){
                    showLoginTab();
                });
                $(".signup-button").click(function(){
                    showSignupTab();
                });

            });
        })();
    </script>
